+++
abstract = "Light fields are able to capture light rays from a scene arriving at different angles, effectively creating multiple perspective views of the same scene. Thus, one of the flagship applications of light fields is to estimate the captured scene geometry, which can notably be achieved by establishing correspondences between the perspective views, usually in the form of a disparity map. Such correspondence estimation has been a long standing research topic in computer vision, with application to stereo vision or optical flow. Research in this area has shown the importance of well designed descriptors to enable fast and accurate matching. We propose in this paper a binary descriptor exploiting the light field gradient over both the spatial and the angular dimensions in order to improve inter view matching. We demonstrate in a disparity estimation application that it can achieve comparable accuracy compared to existing descriptors while being faster to compute."
abstract_short = ""
authors = ["M. Alain", "A. Smolic"]
date = "2020-10-25"
highlight = true
image_preview = ""
math = true
publication = "IEEE International Conference on Image Processing"
publication_short = "ICIP 2020"
publication_types = ["1"]
selected = false
title = "A Spatio-Angular Binary Descriptor for Fast Light Field Inter View Matching"
url_code = ""
url_dataset = ""
url_pdf = "pdf/LF_BOOM_descriptor_camera_ready.pdf"
url_project = ""

<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->

<h2>Presentation</h2>

<iframe width="560" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/SyhGy75BMtc" title="YouTube video player" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen></iframe>



<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2>Additional results</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The proposed Spatio-Angular Binarised Orientation Maps (SABOM) descriptor is compared to SIFT, DAISY, and <a href="https://iis-people.ee.ethz.ch/~michscha/stea/">the original BOOM descriptor</a>.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:heading {"level":3} -->

<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:heading {"level":3} -->
<h3>Visual results</h3>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>We show here comparisons between the disparity maps obtained with the SIFT descriptor and the proposed SABOM descriptor for the <a href="https://lightfield-analysis.uni-konstanz.de/">HCI benchmark</a>, the <a href="http://clim.inria.fr/Datasets/InriaSynLF/index.html">INRIA synthetic dataset</a>, and the <a href="http://lightfield.stanford.edu/lfs.html">Stanford Lego Gantry dataset</a>. As mentioned in the paper, the disparity estimation is used to compare existing descriptors but would require further improvement to compete with the best state-of-the-art method for disparity estimation. The disparity maps are color-coded with <a href="https://ai.googleblog.com/2019/08/turbo-improved-rainbow-colormap-for.html">the Turbo colormap</a>.<br>Overall, similar quality is obtained for both descriptors for while SABOM is much faster to compute.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:heading {"level":4} -->
<h4>Stanford dataset</h4>

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2>Implementation</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The C++ code will soon be available&nbsp;on <a href="https://github.com/V-Sense/">github</a>.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:heading -->
<h2>Additional results</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The proposed Spatio-Angular Binarised Orientation Maps (SABOM) descriptor is compared to SIFT, DAISY, and <a href="https://iis-people.ee.ethz.ch/~michscha/stea/">the original BOOM descriptor</a>.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:heading {"level":3} -->
<h3>ROC performance</h3>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:table -->
<figure class="wp-block-table"><table><tbody><tr><td>HCI dataset</td><td>INRIA Dense dataset</td><td>INRIA Sparse dataset</td></tr><tr><td><a href="https://v-sense.scss.tcd.ie/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/ROC_curve_HCI.png"><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-4476" src="https://v-sense.scss.tcd.ie/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/ROC_curve_HCI-300x225.png" alt="" width="300" height="225"></a></td><td><a href="https://v-sense.scss.tcd.ie/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/ROC_curve_INRIA.png"><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-4477" src="https://v-sense.scss.tcd.ie/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/ROC_curve_INRIA-300x225.png" alt="" width="300" height="225"></a></td><td><a href="https://v-sense.scss.tcd.ie/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/ROC_curve_INRIA_sparse.png"><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-4478" src="https://v-sense.scss.tcd.ie/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/ROC_curve_INRIA_sparse-300x225.png" alt="" width="300" height="225"></a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>
<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:table -->

<!-- /wp:table -->

<!-- wp:heading {"level":3} -->
<h3>Visual results</h3>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>We show here comparisons between the disparity maps obtained with the SIFT descriptor and the proposed SABOM descriptor for the <a href="https://lightfield-analysis.uni-konstanz.de/">HCI benchmark</a>, the <a href="http://clim.inria.fr/Datasets/InriaSynLF/index.html">INRIA synthetic dataset</a>, and the <a href="http://lightfield.stanford.edu/lfs.html">Stanford Lego Gantry dataset</a>. As mentioned in the paper, the disparity estimation is used to compare existing descriptors but would require further improvement to compete with the best state-of-the-art method for disparity estimation. The disparity maps are color-coded with <a href="https://ai.googleblog.com/2019/08/turbo-improved-rainbow-colormap-for.html">the Turbo colormap</a>.<br>Overall, similar quality is obtained for both descriptors for while SABOM is much faster to compute.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<h4>Stanford dataset</h4>
